All Gods
Vasukarс╣Зa V─Бsukra
15 verses: jagat─л, except triс╣гс╣нubh 15
The listing impulse found in the previous hymn is here carried further. The gods in general, groups of gods such as the ─Аdityas, Vasus, and Rudras, and individual gods both major and minor are invoked here, with conventional descriptors and predicates and with standard prayers for help and blessing. There is little to catch the attention in this hymn, though it is certainly competently done.

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬI invoke for the success of the sacrifice the gods, who bestow abundant food, the diffusers of light, theextremely wise who flourish mightily, abounding in all riches, having Indra as their chief, immortal, augmented bysacrifice.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

I call upon the gods of lofty fame for well-beingтАФthe makers of light, attentive to the rite,
who, having all possessions, have grown even stronger, the immortals having Indra as their chief, grown strong through truthтАФ

Griffith

I CALL the Gods of lofty glory for our weal, the makers of the light, well-skilled in sacrifice;
Those who have waxen mightily, Masters of all wealth, Immortal, strengthening Law, the Gods whom Indra leads.

Geldner

Grassmann

Die hochber├╝hmten G├╢tter rufe ich zum Heil, des Lichtes Sch├╢pfer, die des Opfers nehmen wahr, Die alles wissen und zur Macht erwachsen sind, gef├╝hrt von Indra, heilige, unsterbliche.

English translation:

тАЬWe offer praise to the company of the Maruts, the attendants upon Maghavan, who, encouraged byIndra, and instrumental ucted by Varuс╣Зa, have acquired a portion of the light of the sun; the wise worshippers beget thesacrifice.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

Who, thrust forth by Indra, directed forth by Varuс╣Зa, attained a share of the light of the sun.
We would set our thoughts on the community having the Maruts as their troop. In their generosity, they begot the sacrifice as its patrons.

Griffith

For the strong band of Maruts will we frame a hymn: the chiefs shall bring forth sacrifice for Indra’s troop,
Who, sent by Indra and advised by Varuna, have gotten for themselves a share of Surya’s light

Geldner

Grassmann

Die Antheil haben an der Sonne hellem Licht, erregt von Indra und von Varuna belehrt, Dem Schwarm und Heer der Maruts bringen wir Gebet, die F├╝rsten schafften Opfer f├╝r des Indra Schar.

English translation:

тАЬMay Indra with the Vasus guard our dwelling; may Aditi with the ─Аdityas grant us felicity; may thedivine Rudra with the Rudras make us happy;may Tvaс╣гс╣н─Б with the wives of the gods be favourable to us forour prosperity.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

Let Indra with the Vasus protect our livelihood on every side. Let Aditi with the ─Аdityas extend shelter to us.
The god Rudra with the Rudras shall be merciful to us. Let Tvaс╣гс╣нar with the Wives (of the Gods) enliven us for good faring.

Griffith

May Indra with the Vasus keep our dwelling safe, and Aditi with Adityas lend us sure defence.
May the God Rudra with the Rudras favour us, and Tvastar with the Dames further us to success.

English translation:

тАЬAditi, heaven and earth, the mighty Truth (Agni), Indra, Viс╣гс╣Зu, the Maruts, the great sun– (these) weinvoke for our protection, as well as the divine ─Аdityas, the Vasus, the Rudras, and Savit─Б, the accomplisher ofgood works.тАЭ

Griffith

Aditi, Heaven and Earth, the great eternal Law, Indra, Visnu, the Maruts, and the lofty Sky.
We call upon Adityas, on the Gods, for help, on Vasus, Rudras, Savitar of wondrous deeds.

Griffith

Lords of all wealth, Immortal, furtherers of prayer, grant us a triply-guarding refuge from distress.

рдкрджрд╛рд░реНрдерд╛рдиреНрд╡рдпрднрд╛рд╖рд╛рдГ - (рдзреАрднрд┐рдГ рд╕рд░рд╕реНрд╡рд╛рдиреН) рдХрд░реНрдорднрд┐рдГ тАЬрдзреАрдГ рдХрд░реНрдордирд╛рдотАЭ [рдирд┐рдШрежрелредрез] рдпреЛ рдЬреНрдЮрд╛рдирд╡рд╛рдиреН рдкреНрд░рд╛рдкреНрддрдЬреНрдЮрд╛рдирдГ (рд╡рд░реБрдгрдГ) рд╡рд░рдпрд┐рддрд╛ рдЙрдкрджреЗрд╢рдХрдГ (рдзреГрддрд╡реНрд░рддрдГ рдкреВрд╖рд╛) рдзреГрддрд╕рдЩреНрдХрд▓реНрдкрдГ рдХреГрддрд╕рдЩреНрдХрд▓реНрдкреЛ рджреГрдврд╕рдЩреНрдХрд▓реНрдкреЛ рд╡рд╛ рдкрд╛рд▓рдХреЛ рд░рд╛рдЬрд╛ (рдорд╣рд┐рдорд╛ рд╡рд┐рд╖реНрдгреБрдГ) рд╕реНрд╡рдорд╣рддреНрддреНрд╡реЗрди рд╡реНрдпрд╛рдкрдХрдГ рдкрд░рдорд╛рддреНрдорд╛ (рд╡рд╛рдпреБрдГ) рдкреБрд░реЛрд╣рд┐рддрдГ тАЬрд╡рд╛рдпреБрд░реНрд╡рд╛рд╡ рдкреБрд░реЛрд╣рд┐рддрдГтАЭ [рдРрежреоредреи] (рдЕрд╢реНрд╡рд┐рдирд╛) рд╕реБрд╢рд┐рдХреНрд╖рд┐рддреМ рд╕реНрддреНрд░реАрдкреБрд░реБрд╖реМ тАЬрдЕрд╢реНрд╡рд┐рдирд╛ рд╕реБрд╢рд┐рдХреНрд╖рд┐рддреМ рд╕реНрддреНрд░реАрдкреБрд░реБрд╖реМтАЭ [рдпрдЬреБрежрейреоредрезреирджрдпрд╛рдирдиреНрджрдГ] (рдмреНрд░рд╣реНрдордХреГрддрдГ) рдмреНрд░рд╣реНрдордЬреНрдЮрд╛рдирд╛рдзреНрдпрд╛рдкрдХрд╛рдГ (рдЕрдореГрддрд╛рдГ) рдЬреАрд╡рдиреНрдореБрдХреНрддрд╛рдГ (рд╡рд┐рд╢реНрд╡рд╡реЗрджрд╕рдГ) рдкреНрд░рд╡реЗрд╖реНрдЯрд╡реНрдпрдЬреНрдЮрд╛рдирд╡рдиреНрддрдГ (рдирдГ) рдЕрд╕реНрдорднреНрдпрдВ (рдЕрдВрд╣рд╕рдГ) рдкрд╛рдкрд╛рддреН рдкрд╛рдкрд╕рдореНрдкрд░реНрдХрддрдГ-рд╕рдВрд╕рд╛рд░рд╛рддреН рдкрд╛рд░рдВ (рддреНрд░рд┐рд╡рд░реВрдердВ рд╢рд░реНрдо рдпрдВрд╕рдиреН) рддреНрд░реАрдгрд┐-рдЖрдзреНрдпрд╛рддреНрдорд┐рдХрд╛рдзрд┐рджреИрд╡рд┐рдХрд╛рдзрд┐рднреМрддрд┐рдХрджреБрдГрдЦрд╡рд╛рд░рдХрдВ рд╕реБрдЦрдВ рд╢рд░рдгрдВ рд╡рд╛ рдкреНрд░рдпрдЪреНрдЫрдиреНрддреБ реерелрее

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬMay our sacrifice be the showerer (of benefits); may the gods who are worthy of sacrifice be theshowerers (of benefits); may the priest, may the presenters of the oblation, be the showerers (of benefits); mayheaven and earth receiving adoration be the showerers (of benefits); may Parjanya be the showerer (of rain);may those who praise (the gods) with showers be showerers.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

Let our sacrifice be a bull and those belonging to the sacrifice bulls, the gods bulls, and those making the oblation bulls;
truthful Heaven and Earth bulls, Parjanya a bull, and those praising the bull bulls.

Griffith

Strong be the sacrifice, strong be the Holy Ones, strong the preparers of oblation, strong the Gods.
Mighty be Heaven and Earth, true to eternal Law, strong be Parjanya, strong be they who laud the Strong.

Geldner

Bullenhaft ist das Opfer, bullenhaft m├╝ssen die Opferw├╝rdigen sein, bullenhaft die G├╢tter, bullenhaft die Opferbereiter. Bullenhaft sind Himmel und Erde, die ordnungsvollen, bullenhaft Parjanya, bullenhaft die wie die Bullen Singenden.

Grassmann

Stier sei das Opfer, Stiere die ehrw├╝rdigen, die G├╢tter Stiere, Stiere die das Opfer weihn, Und Stiere Erd’ und Himmel, sie die heiligen, ein Stier Pardschanja, Stier, wer G├╢tter-Stiere preist,

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬI glorify for the obtaining of food the two showerers (of benefits), Agni and Soma, the many-laudedshowerers (of benefits), may these two whom the priests have worshipped with divine worship bestow upon us atriply-guarded dwelling.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

I entreat the bulls Agni and Soma in order to win the prize, those two bulls lauded by many.
Those two to whom the bulls have sacrificed through their sacrifice
to the gods, those two will spread out shelter providing threefold
defense for us.

Griffith

To win us strength I glorify the Mighty Twain, Agni and Soma, Mighty Ones whom many laud.
May these vouchsafe us shelter with a triple guard, these whom the strong have served in worship of the Gods.

Geldner

Agni und Soma, den Bullenhaften, rede ich zu, um den Preis zu gewinnen, den beiden vielgelobten Bullen, denen die Bullen mit G├╢tteropfer geopfert haben, die sollen uns dreifach sch├╝tzende Zuflucht gew├дhren.

Grassmann

Die Stiere, Agni, Soma, rufe ich herbei, die vielger├╝hmten Stiere, Labung zu empfahn, Die von den Stieren sind geehrt durch Gottesdienst; so reichet uns denn Schutzwehr, welche dreifach, schirmt.

English translation:

тАЬThe (gods) observing obligations endowed with vigour, developers of sacrifice, possessed ofabundant brightness, the defenders of sacrifices, having Agni for their priest, enjoying truth, unassailable, setfree the waters at the combat with the Vс╣Ыtra.тАЭ

Vigour: kс╣гatriyaс╕е = of the kс╣гatriya clan; or, strong

Jamison Brereton

The rulers whose commandments are upheld, who bring forth the sacrifice, heaven-lofty ones, the full glory of the rite,
whose Hotar is Agni, who serve the truth without deceitтАФthey let loose the waters following on the triumph over Vr╠еtra.

Griffith

Potent, with firm-fixt laws, arranging sacrifice, visiting solemn rites in splendour of the day,
Obeying Order, these whose priest is Agni, free from falsehood, poured the waters out when Vrtra died.

Geldner

Die Herrscher, die die Gesetze aufrecht erhalten, das Opfer einrichten, im hohen Himmel wohnen, die Oberherren des Opfers, mit Agni als Hotri, der Wahrheit Pfleger, die Truglosen, sie lie├Яen die Gew├дsser laufen nach ├Ьberwindung des Vritra.

Grassmann

Gesetzbeschirmer, Herrscher, Opferschm├╝ckende, die himmlischen Versch├╢nrer jedes Opferfests, Des Werkes Pfleger, deren Priester Agni ist, die holden machten Wasser frei im Vritrakampf.

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬThe gods engendered the heaven and earth with their respective functions, the waters, the plural nts, thesacred trees; they filled the whole firmament (with lustre) for its protection; they graced the desirable (sacrifice) intheir own person ns.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

They begot heaven and earth to their commandments, and the waters, the plants, and the trees belonging to the sacrifice.
They filled the midspace and the sun to give help. The gods clasped
their will to themselves.

Griffith

The Holy Ones engendered, for their several laws, the heavens and earth, the waters, and the plants and trees.
They filled the firmament with heavenly light for help: the Gods embodied Wish and made it beautiful.

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬMay the upholders of the sky, the radiant with truth, the well-armed deities, V─Бta and Parjanya, (theutterers) of the mighty thunder, the waters, the plural nts, amplify our praises; may the liberal Bhaga and V─Бjinscome to my invocation.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

The radiant with truth: с╣Ъbhus;

Suhastaс╕е = dexterous, having their hands furnished withgood weapons, thunderbolts and the like;

V─Бjins = Agni;

V─Бyu = the sun: Taittir─лya Br─Бhmaс╣Зa 1.6.3.9

Jamison Brereton

Let the upholders of heaven, the R╠еbhus with skilled hands, let V─Бta and Parjanya, (masters?) of Thunder the buffalo,
let the waters and plants advance our songs. Let Bhaga, Gift, and the prizewinners come to my call.

Griffith

May they who bear up heaven, the Rbhus deft of hand, and Vata and Parjanya of the thundering Bull,
The waters and the plants, promote the songs we sing: come Bhaga, Rati, and the Vaijns to my call.

English translation:

тАЬMay the flowing Sindhu, the atmosphere, the firmament, Aja Ekap─Бd, the rain-bearing thunder-cloud,and Ahirbudhnya hear my words; may the wise universal gods (listen to) my (praises).тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

The sea, the river, the dusky realm, the midspace; Aja Ekapad,
Thundering, the flood,
and Ahi Budhnya will hear my words, (also) all the gods and my
patrons.

Griffith

Sindhu, the sea, the region, and the firmament, the thunder, and the ocean, Aja-Ekapad,
The Dragon of the Deep, shall listen to my words, and all the Deities and Princes shall give ear.

Das Meer, die Sindhu, der Umkreis, die Luft, der ungeborene Einfu├Я, der Donnerschlag, die Wasserflut, der Drache der Tiefe erh├╢re meine Worte, alle G├╢tter und meine freigebigen Patrone!

Grassmann

Der Ocean, der Strom, der weite Raum, die Luft, der Kreiselwind, der donnernde, der wogende, Der Wetterdrache h├╢re meiner Lieder Schall, die G├╢tter alle und die Gl├дnzenden mein Wort.

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬMay we men be (diligent in providing) for your food, (O gods); conduct our ancient sacrifice to asuccessful end, ─Аdityas, Rudras, and genitive rous Vasus, graciously accept these hymns which are being recited.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

Might we (all) be Manus [=like Manu] for you, to pursue the gods. Lead our sacrifice forth toward the east straight to the goal.
O ─Аdityas, Rudras, and Vasus, of good gifts, give life to these sacred formulations as they are being recited.

Griffith

May we, be yours, we men, to entertain the Gods: further our sacrifice and give it full success.

English translation:

тАЬI follow the two chief priests the divine offerers of burnt sacrifices, (I follow) successfully the path ofsacrifice; we solicit (wealth of) the contiguous lord of the field, and the immortal and not unheeding universaldeities.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

The two chief priests: i.e., Agni and ─Аditya]. well-being; having come to us, gods, at our desire, bestow wealth upon us like affectionate relations.

Jamison Brereton

The two divine Hotars, the first two set in front, do I follow along the path of truth straight to the goal.
We beseech the lord of the field, our neighbor, and all the immortal
gods, who do not stay distant.

Griffith

I follow with success upon the path of Law the two celestial Hotars, Priests of oldest time.
We pray to him who dwelleth near, Guard of the Field, to all Immortal Gods who never are remiss.

Jamison Brereton

The Vasiс╣гс╣нhas have made speech in the manner of their father, invoking the gods in the manner of that seer for well-being.
Like pleased kinsmen, coming here at our desire, shake good things
down upon us, o gods.

Griffith

Vasistha’s sons have raised their voices, like their sire. Rsi-like praying to the Gods for happiness.
Like friendly-minded kinsmen, come at our desire, O Gods, and shake down treasures on us from above.

тАЬ(Descendant of) Vasiс╣гс╣нha, I have glorified the immortal gods who preside over all the worlds; maythey this day bestow upon us widely-famed food; do you always cherish us with blessings.тАЭ

Vasiс╣гс╣нha has extolled the immortal gods, who stand out over all living beings.
Let them grant us wide-ranging space today. тАУ Do you protect us
always with your blessings.
The two hymns of Ay─Бsya ─Ас╣Еgirasa (67тАУ68) are particularly noteworthy treatments of Br╠еhaspati and the Vala myth.

May they this day grant us wide space and freedom: ye Gods, preserve us evermore with blessings.

рдкрджрд╛рд░реНрдерд╛рдиреНрд╡рдпрднрд╛рд╖рд╛рдГ - (рд╡рд╕рд┐рд╖реНрдардГ) рд╕рд░реНрд╡рд╡рд┐рд╖рдпреЗрд╖реБ рд╡рд╕рд┐рддреГрддрдордГ (рдЕрдореГрддрд╛рдиреН рджреЗрд╡рд╛рдиреН) рдЬреАрд╡рдиреНрдореБрдХреНрддрд╛рдиреН рд╡рд┐рджреБрд╖рдГ (рд╡рд╡рдиреНрджреЗ) рдЕрднрд┐рд╡рдиреНрджрддрд┐ (рдпреЗ рд╡рд┐рд╢реНрд╡рд╛ рднреБрд╡рдирд╛-рдЕрднрд┐ рдкреНрд░рддрд╕реНрдереБрдГ) рдпреЗ рдЬреАрд╡рдиреНрдореБрдХреНрддрд╛рдГ рд╕рд░реНрд╡рд╛рдгрд┐ рдЬреНрдЮрд╛рдирд╛рдирд┐-рдЕрдзрд┐рдХрд╛рд░реЗрдг рдкреНрд░рддрд┐рд╖реНрдардиреНрддрд┐ (рддреЗ) рддреЗ рдЦрд▓реБ (рдирдГ) рдЕрд╕реНрдорднреНрдпрдореН (рдЕрджреНрдп) рдЕрд╕реНрдорд┐рдиреН рдХрд╛рд▓реЗ рдЬреАрд╡рдиреЗ (рдЙрд░реБрдЧрд╛рдпрдВ рд░рд╛рд╕рдиреНрддрд╛рдореН) рдмрд╣реБрдкреНрд░рд╢рдВрд╕рдиреАрдпрдВ рдЬреНрдЮрд╛рдирдВ рдкрд░рдорд╛рддреНрдордЬреНрдЮрд╛рдирдВ рдкреНрд░рдпрдЪреНрдЫрддреБ (рдпреВрдпрдВ рд╕реНрд╡рд╕реНрддрд┐рднрд┐рдГ-рдирдГ рд╕рджрд╛ рдкрд╛рдд) рд╣реЗ рд╡рд┐рджреНрд╡рд╛рдВрд╕реЛ ! рдпреВрдпрдВ рдХрд▓реНрдпрд╛рдгрд╡рдЪрдиреИрд░рд╕реНрдорд╛рдиреН рд╕рджрд╛ рд░рдХреНрд╖рдд реерезрелрее
